Sarangworld Traceroute Project Known Hostname Codes

Below is a list of codes and IP addresses I can translate into city names with latitudes and longitudes (for mapping purposes). The list is nowhere near complete, and sometimes reflects a "best guess" on my part. For example, I guessed the "EWR" stood for "Newark, NJ, USA", because EWR is the airport code for that airport in that city. It's possible some of my guesses are wrong (as another example, I guessed "lnmtco" stood for "Longmont, Colorado, USA" because CO is the state code for Colorado and Longmont is the largest city in Colorado that could conceivably be abbreviated "lnmt"-- but, as you can see, that's a bit of a longshot). As a final note, "ana" translates to "Anaheim, CA, USA" because the ISP using that code actually gave me this translation (plus a few others). IP address data is primarily from APNIC.

Additionally, all U.S. cities and states in the Census Bureau's Gazetteer are recognized in the form "cityname.st" (eg, "boston.ma" is recognized to be Boston, Massachusetts), but are not listed here. Cities with multiple-word names are recognized as though the words were separated by hyphens (eg, "corpus-christi.tx" is recognized to be Corpus Christi, TX). As of January 1, 2003, I use the Census 2000 data. As of 15 Feb 2004, "st.cityname" is also recogized (eg, "ma.boston" is also recognized as Boston, Massachusetts).
